% The next line sets Emoji as non-Japanese characters in LuaTeX-ja
% æ¬¡ã®è¡Œã¯çµµæ–‡å­—ã‚’æ¬§æ–‡æ‰±ã„ã¨ã—ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã€‚ãã†ã—ãªã„ã¨çµµæ–‡å­—ã‚’å’Œæ–‡ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ³ãƒˆã‹ã‚‰æ¢ã—ã¦è¡¨ç¤ºã—ãªã„
\ltjsetparameter{jacharrange={-33}}

\newcounter{myline}
\stepcounter{myline}
\newcommand{\mylinecount}{\arabic{myline}\stepcounter{myline}}

\setmainfont[RawFeature={+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Symbol}
\newcommand{\fontA}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf;+dist;+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Emoji} #1}}
\newcommand{\fontB}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf;+dist;+ccmp}]{Noto Color Emoji} #1}}
\newcommand{\fontC}[1]{{\coloremoji*{#1}}}
\newcommand{\fontD}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf;+ccmp}]{Twemoji Mozilla} #1}}


\begin{document}
\noindent
List all emoji in Unicode 12.0 by HarfLaTeX + LuaTeX-ja\\
Built from https://unicode.org/emoji/charts/emoji-list.html\\
Twitter color SVG opentype font https://github.com/eosrei/twemoji-color-font/releases cannot be used in color as far as I know. But Twitter Emoji can be used by BXcoloremoji\\ https://github.com/zr-tex8r/BXcoloremoji\\
Twitter font in COLR format is from https://github.com/mozilla/twemoji-colr
